## <a name="windows-server-2012-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="94d88-2093">Attributs Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="94d88-2093">Windows Server 2012 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="94d88-2094">Cette classe contient les attributs suivants pour Windows Server 2012 :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="94d88-2094">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
